lower_house_form_effect_relative_power = {
	base = 1
	complex_trigger_modifier = {
		trigger = count_galcom_member
		parameters = {
			limit = {
				relative_power = { who = prev value >= superior }
			}
		}
		potential = {
			count_galcom_member = {
				limit = {
					relative_power = { who = prev value >= superior }
				}
				count > 2
			}
		}
		mode = multiply
		mult = 0.5
	}
	complex_trigger_modifier = {
		trigger = count_galcom_member
		parameters = {
			limit = {
				relative_power = { who = prev value <= pathetic }
			}
		}
		potential = {
			count_galcom_member = {
				limit = {
					relative_power = { who = prev value <= pathetic }
				}
				count > 2
			}
		}
		mode = divide
		mult = 0.5
	}
	modifier = {
		mult = 3
		OR = {
			is_galactic_custodian = yes
			is_galactic_emperor = yes
		}
	}
	modifier = {
		mult = 2
		is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
		is_galactic_custodian = no
		is_galactic_emperor = no
	}
	max = 10
	min = 0.1
}

	base = 1
	modifier = {
		add = 2
		OR = {

			is_galactic_emperor = yes
		}
	}
	modifier = {
		add = 1
		is_part_of_galactic_council = yes

	}

@resolution_weight_hated = 3
@resolution_weight_disliked = 4
@resolution_weight_unpopular = 5
@resolution_weight_normal = 6
@resolution_weight_popular = 6.5
@resolution_weight_loved = 7

proposer_opinion_factor = {
	base = 1000
	complex_trigger_modifier = {
		potential = {
			NOT = { is_same_value = event_target:proposer_$resolution$ }
			opinion = {
				who = event_target:proposer_$resolution$
				value > 0
			}
		}
		trigger = opinion
		parameters = {
			who = event_target:proposer_$resolution$
		}
		mode = add
		mult = 0.4
	}
	complex_trigger_modifier = {
		potential = {
			NOT = { is_same_value = event_target:proposer_$resolution$ }
			opinion = {
				who = event_target:proposer_$resolution$
				value < 0
			}
		}
		trigger = opinion
		parameters = {
			who = event_target:proposer_$resolution$
		}
		mode = add
		mult = 0.667
	}
	modifier = {
		is_same_value = event_target:proposer_$resolution$
		add = 300
	}
	divide = 1000
	min = 0.5
	max = 1.3
}

		desc = civic_environmentalist

		factor = 0.25
		has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
		desc = civic_agrarian_idyll
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 2
		OR = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_mining_guilds
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_rockbreakers
		}
		desc = gal_com_miner_civic
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 1.2
		country_uses_food = no
		desc = gal_com_country_uses_food_no
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 1.2
		is_lithoid_empire = yes
		desc = lithoid
	}

	modifier = { #proposer_opinion_factor

	}
}

		is_authoritarian = yes
		desc = ethic_authoritarian
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 0.5
		has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
		desc = civic_agrarian_idyll
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 0.5
		has_valid_civic = civic_free_haven
		desc = civic_free_haven
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 0.5
		has_valid_civic = civic_idealistic_foundation
		desc = civic_idealistic_foundation
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 0.5
		has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection
		desc = civic_inwards_perfection
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 0.5
		has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
		desc = civic_machine_servitor
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 2
		OR = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_slaver_guilds
			has_valid_civic = civic_indentured_assets
			is_slaver = yes
		}
		desc = gal_com_slaver_empire
	}

	
	modifier = { #proposer_opinion_factor

			has_civic = civic_machine_servitor
		}
		desc = gal_com_opposing_civics
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 1.2
		is_authoritarian = yes
		desc = ethic_authoritarian
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 2
		OR = {
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			AND = {
				is_subject = yes
				overlord = {
					opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
					is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				}
			}
		}
		desc = gal_com_they_or_overlord_on_galatic_council
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 0.8
		galactic_community_rank > 5
		NAND = {
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = {
				opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			}
		}
		desc = gal_com_they_nor_overlord_not_on_galatic_council
	}
	
	modifier = { #proposer_opinion_factor
		factor = value:proposer_opinion_factor|resolution|resolution_community_champions|
	}

	weight = @resolution_weight_loved	#wil, note (made after the below): the level 1 has tons of benefits actually (2 starbases!!, 5 base trade protection, +5%unity, +5%admin cap)
	
	#was @resolution_weight_normal		#Significant Costs for everyone		#wil, note: if so, this should be changed; every level 1 resolution is weight_loved, and flavorwise EVERY nation would like some matter of "our sovereignty is respected"; by which i mean, we ought to come up with better tradeoffs for this tree, to make it more appealing for empires to slide into xenophobic tendencies (Galactic Community should not just be about strangling weaker empires with bad effects for them; it should in large part be about slowly compelling others to adopt your empire's ethos, mindset, and standards of 'decency,' however that may be defined

	modifier = {
		factor = 2.5
		is_xenophobe = yes 
	}
	modifier = {
		factor = 2.5
		has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection 
	}
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.9		#was 0.3, xenophiles do not actually hate this that much; the positive effects outweigh the diplocost and trade hits
		OR = {
			is_xenophile = yes
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = multispecies 
		}
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 0.9		#hyper-trade empires do care about any hit to it, but 2 starbases and their trade hubs may make up for it
		OR = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_merchant_guilds
			is_megacorp = yes #Trade-heavy empires don't like - trade value
			
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 1.2
		is_militarist = yes 
	}							#both of these like the starbase increase, as either anchorages for mil or defensive points for pac
	modifier = {
		factor = 1.2
		is_pacifist = yes
	}
	
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 3		#was 1.1
		is_gestalt = yes
		#This resolution does less for gestalts, but not nothing 	#wil, note: for gestalts, this res is basically 2 free starbases, admin cap buff (very useful for MIs), and unity, essentially for free
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.9
		has_valid_civic = civic_hive_empath		#wil, note: empaths care a bit
	}

	
	modifier = { #proposer_opinion_factor
		factor = value:proposer_opinion_factor|resolution|resolution_guarded_sovereignty|
	}
}

		is_spiritualist = yes
		#wil, note: once spiritualists start tomb-raiding, they declare artifacts to be miraculous relics (see their minor artifact option)
	}

		OR = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_memorialist
			has_valid_civic = civic_hive_memorialist
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_memorialist
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {			#get lots of minerals anyway
		factor = 0.8
		OR = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_mining_guilds
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_rockbreakers
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {			#need lots of minerals
		factor = 1.2
		is_lithoid_empire = yes
	}
	
	modifier = {			#have no source of artifacts
		factor = 0.8
		has_country_resource = {
			type = minor_artifacts
			amount < 100
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {			#have a use for lots of artifacts
		factor = 0.8
		has_technology = "tech_arcane_deciphering"
	}
	
	#would like to add some "make sure this won't crash the voter's economy" code
	
	modifier = { #proposer_opinion_factor
		factor = value:proposer_opinion_factor|resolution|resolution_discovery_archeology_repeal_2|
	}

lhw_resolution_sanctions_tech_repeal_4 = {
	weight = @resolution_weight_loved		#was unpopular
	
	#wil, note: weights completely reworked, in part to no longer be ultra-stupid -- previously was 0.25 OPPOSED by materialists not in breach, despite them being the most likely to be hurt by the sanctions at some future date
	#other vanilla ones were 2 if in breach, 2 if fedallies in breach, 0.75 if rival in breach
	
	#these weights are an attempt to both fix that and make sanctions depend more on who will (or who will likely eventually) be affected by them
	#they may very well need adjusting

	modifier = {										
		factor = 5
		OR = {
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			has_modifier = resolution_denounced
		}
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 5
		any_federation_ally = {
			OR = {
				is_in_breach_of_any = yes
				has_modifier = resolution_denounced
			}
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.25
		any_rival_country = {
			OR = {
				is_in_breach_of_any = yes
				has_modifier = resolution_denounced
			}
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.25
		has_valid_civic = civic_cutthroat_politics			
		#wil, note: i like flavor-focused weights like this
		NOR = {
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			has_modifier = resolution_denounced
		}
	}
	
	##########################
	#sanction-specific stuff:#
	##########################
	
	modifier = {										
		factor = 20
		OR = {
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			has_modifier = resolution_denounced
		}
		OR = {
			is_materialist = yes
			has_valid_civic = civic_hive_natural_neural_network
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_introspective
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_predictive_analysis
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 2
		OR = { 
			is_materialist = yes
			has_valid_civic = civic_hive_natural_neural_network
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_introspective

		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 1.2
		OR = { 
			has_valid_civic = civic_technocracy
			has_origin = origin_mechanists
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.7
		is_spiritualist = yes
		NOR = {
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			has_modifier = resolution_denounced
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {

				has_valid_civic = civic_hive_natural_neural_network
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_introspective
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_predictive_analysis
			}
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.5
		any_rival_country = {
			OR = {
				is_materialist = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_hive_natural_neural_network
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_introspective

			}
		}
		NOR = {
			is_materialist = yes
			has_valid_civic = civic_hive_natural_neural_network

lhw_resolution_sanctions_administrative_repeal_4 = {
	weight = @resolution_weight_loved		#was unpopular
	
	#wil, note: weights completely reworked, in part to no longer be ultra-stupid -- previously was 0.25 OPPOSED by xenophiles and diplomatic types not in breach, despite them being the most likely to be hurt by the sanctions at some future date
	#0.25 if xenophile, diplomatic corps, public relations experts, empath, servitors, OR on the galactic council
	#other vanilla ones were 2 if in breach, 2 if fedallies in breach, 0.75 if rival in breach
	
	#these weights are an attempt to both fix that and make sanctions depend more on who will (or who will likely eventually) be affected by them
	#they may very well need adjusting

	modifier = {										
		factor = 5
		OR = {
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			has_modifier = resolution_denounced
		}
	}

	modifier = {
		factor = 5
		any_federation_ally = {
			OR = {
				is_in_breach_of_any = yes
				has_modifier = resolution_denounced
			}
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.25
		any_rival_country = {
			OR = {
				is_in_breach_of_any = yes
				has_modifier = resolution_denounced
			}
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.25
		has_valid_civic = civic_cutthroat_politics			
		#wil, note: i like flavor-focused weights like this
		NOR = {
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			has_modifier = resolution_denounced
		}
	}
	
	##########################
	#sanction-specific stuff:#
	##########################
	
	modifier = {										
		factor = 20
		OR = {
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			has_modifier = resolution_denounced
		}
		OR = { 
			is_xenophile = yes
			is_megacorp = yes
			has_valid_civic = civic_hive_empath
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			has_ai_personality = federation_builders
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 2
		OR = { 
			is_xenophile = yes
			is_megacorp = yes
			has_valid_civic = civic_hive_empath
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			has_ai_personality = federation_builders
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 1.2
		OR = { 
			has_valid_civic = civic_diplomatic_corps
			has_valid_civic = civic_public_relations_specialists
			is_machine_empire = yes #as they already have a sprawl penalty to deal with
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.7
		OR = {
			is_xenophobe = yes
			has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_supremacist
			has_federation = no
		}
		NOR = {
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			has_modifier = resolution_denounced
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.8
		OR = { 
			has_valid_civic = civic_efficient_bureaucracy
			has_valid_civic = civic_byzantine_bureaucracy
			has_authority = auth_hive_mind
			has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection
		}
		NOR = {
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			has_modifier = resolution_denounced
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 1.5
		any_federation_ally = {
			OR = { 
				is_xenophile = yes
				is_megacorp = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_hive_empath
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
				has_ai_personality = federation_builders
			}
		}
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.5
		any_rival_country = {
			OR = { 
				is_xenophile = yes
				is_megacorp = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_hive_empath

				has_ai_personality = federation_builders
			}
		}

		desc = ethic_egalitarian
	}

		desc = ethic_egalitarian
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 3
		is_civic_shared_burden = yes
		desc = civic_shared_burden
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 2
		is_civic_has_meritocracy = yes
		desc = gal_com_meritocracy_civic
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 2
		OR = {
			has_authority = auth_democratic
			has_authority = auth_cooperative
		}
		desc = auth_democratic
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 1.25
		OR = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			is_civic_free_haven = yes
			is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
		}
		desc = gal_com_supporting_civics
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.5
		OR = {
			has_authority = auth_imperial
			has_authority = auth_dictatorial
			has_authority = auth_private
		}
		desc = gal_com_autocrat
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.5
		is_gestalt = yes
		is_open_gestalt = no
		is_civic_machine_servitor = no
		desc = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
	}
	
	modifier = {

			is_civic_authoritarian = yes
		}
		desc = auth_authoritarian
	}
	
	modifier = {

			is_slaver = yes

		}
		desc = gal_com_slaver_empire
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.75
		any_owned_planet = {
			planet_crime > 30
		}
		desc = gal_com_owns_high_crime_planet
	}
	
	modifier = {
		factor = 0.75
		any_owned_planet = {
			has_branch_office = yes
			exists = branch_office_owner
			branch_office_owner = { is_criminal_syndicate = yes }
		}
		desc = gal_com_owns_planet_with_criminal_syndicate_branch_office
	}

	
	modifier = { #proposer_opinion_factor
